[30;1m2 | [0m[35m======================[0m

[30;1m288 | [0m[35mIn YAQL there are no built-in operators. The parser is given a list of all[0m
[30;1m289 | [0m[35mpossible operator names (symbols), their associativity, precedence, and type,[0m
[30;1m290 | [0m[35mbut it knows nothing about what operators are applicable for what operands.[0m
[30;1m291 | [0m[35mEach time a parser recognizes the ``X OP Y`` construct and `OP` is a known[0m
[30;1m292 | [0m[35mbinary operator name, it translates the expression to ``#operator_OP(X, Y)``.[0m
[30;1m293 | [0m[35mThus. ``2 + 3`` becomes ``#operator_+(2, 3)`` where `#operator_+` is an[0m
[30;1m294 | [0m[35mimplicit function with several implementations including the one for number[0m
